<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
<s> thus when he spoke it was in a sharper voice as if he had been awakened from a pleasant dream <\s>
<s> what d'you do with yourself all day <\s>
<s> you never come round to park lane <\s>
<s> she seemed to be making very lame excuses and james did not look at her <\s>
<s> he did not want to believe that she was really avoiding them it would mean too much <\s>
<s> i expect the fact is you haven't time he said you're always about with june <\s>
<s> i expect you're useful to her with her young man chaperoning and one thing and another <\s>
<s> they tell me she's never at home now your uncle jolyon he doesn't like it i fancy being left so much alone as he is <\s>
<s> they tell me she's always hanging about for this young bosinney i suppose he comes here every day <\s>
<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>

<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>
<s> james rose and took a turn with bent head <\s>
<s> that's it he said you young people you all stick together you all think you know best <\s>
<s> halting his tall lank figure before her he raised a finger and levelled it at her bosom as though bringing an indictment against her beauty all i can say is these artistic people or whatever they call themselves they're as unreliable as they can be and my advice to you is don't you have too much to do with him <\s>
<s> irene smiled and in the curve of her lips was a strange provocation <\s>
<s> she seemed to have lost her deference <\s>
<s> her breast rose and fell as though with secret anger she drew her hands inwards from their rest on the arms of her chair until the tips of her fingers met and her dark eyes looked unfathomably at james <\s>
<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>

<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
<s> thus when he spoke it was in a sharper voice as if he had been awakened from a pleasant dream <\s>
<s> what d'you do with yourself all day <\s>
<s> you never come round to park lane <\s>
<s> she seemed to be making very lame excuses and james did not look at her <\s>
<s> he did not want to believe that she was really avoiding them it would mean too much <\s>
<s> i expect the fact is you haven't time he said you're always about with june <\s>
<s> i expect you're useful to her with her young man chaperoning and one thing and another <\s>
<s> they tell me she's never at home now your uncle jolyon he doesn't like it i fancy being left so much alone as he is <\s>
<s> they tell me she's always hanging about for this young bosinney i suppose he comes here every day <\s>
<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>
<s> james rose and took a turn with bent head <\s>
<s> that's it he said you young people you all stick together you all think you know best <\s>
<s> halting his tall lank figure before her he raised a finger and levelled it at her bosom as though bringing an indictment against her beauty all i can say is these artistic people or whatever they call themselves they're as unreliable as they can be and my advice to you is don't you have too much to do with him <\s>
<s> irene smiled and in the curve of her lips was a strange provocation <\s>
<s> she seemed to have lost her deference <\s>
<s> her breast rose and fell as though with secret anger she drew her hands inwards from their rest on the arms of her chair until the tips of her fingers met and her dark eyes looked unfathomably at james <\s>
<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>

<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
<s> thus when he spoke it was in a sharper voice as if he had been awakened from a pleasant dream <\s>
<s> what d'you do with yourself all day <\s>
<s> you never come round to park lane <\s>
<s> she seemed to be making very lame excuses and james did not look at her <\s>
<s> he did not want to believe that she was really avoiding them it would mean too much <\s>
<s> i expect the fact is you haven't time he said you're always about with june <\s>
<s> i expect you're useful to her with her young man chaperoning and one thing and another <\s>
<s> they tell me she's never at home now your uncle jolyon he doesn't like it i fancy being left so much alone as he is <\s>
<s> they tell me she's always hanging about for this young bosinney i suppose he comes here every day <\s>
<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>
<s> james rose and took a turn with bent head <\s>
<s> that's it he said you young people you all stick together you all think you know best <\s>
<s> halting his tall lank figure before her he raised a finger and levelled it at her bosom as though bringing an indictment against her beauty all i can say is these artistic people or whatever they call themselves they're as unreliable as they can be and my advice to you is don't you have too much to do with him <\s>
<s> irene smiled and in the curve of her lips was a strange provocation <\s>
<s> she seemed to have lost her deference <\s>
<s> her breast rose and fell as though with secret anger she drew her hands inwards from their rest on the arms of her chair until the tips of her fingers met and her dark eyes looked unfathomably at james <\s>
<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>

<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
<s> thus when he spoke it was in a sharper voice as if he had been awakened from a pleasant dream <\s>
<s> what d'you do with yourself all day <\s>
<s> you never come round to park lane <\s>
<s> she seemed to be making very lame excuses and james did not look at her <\s>
<s> he did not want to believe that she was really avoiding them it would mean too much <\s>
<s> i expect the fact is you haven't time he said you're always about with june <\s>
<s> i expect you're useful to her with her young man chaperoning and one thing and another <\s>
<s> they tell me she's never at home now your uncle jolyon he doesn't like it i fancy being left so much alone as he is <\s>
<s> they tell me she's always hanging about for this young bosinney i suppose he comes here every day <\s>
<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>
<s> james rose and took a turn with bent head <\s>
<s> that's it he said you young people you all stick together you all think you know best <\s>
<s> halting his tall lank figure before her he raised a finger and levelled it at her bosom as though bringing an indictment against her beauty all i can say is these artistic people or whatever they call themselves they're as unreliable as they can be and my advice to you is don't you have too much to do with him <\s>
<s> irene smiled and in the curve of her lips was a strange provocation <\s>
<s> she seemed to have lost her deference <\s>
<s> her breast rose and fell as though with secret anger she drew her hands inwards from their rest on the arms of her chair until the tips of her fingers met and her dark eyes looked unfathomably at james <\s>
<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>

<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
<s> thus when he spoke it was in a sharper voice as if he had been awakened from a pleasant dream <\s>
<s> what d'you do with yourself all day <\s>
<s> you never come round to park lane <\s>
<s> she seemed to be making very lame excuses and james did not look at her <\s>
<s> he did not want to believe that she was really avoiding them it would mean too much <\s>
<s> i expect the fact is you haven't time he said you're always about with june <\s>
<s> i expect you're useful to her with her young man chaperoning and one thing and another <\s>
<s> they tell me she's never at home now your uncle jolyon he doesn't like it i fancy being left so much alone as he is <\s>
<s> they tell me she's always hanging about for this young bosinney i suppose he comes here every day <\s>
<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>
<s> james rose and took a turn with bent head <\s>
<s> that's it he said you young people you all stick together you all think you know best <\s>
<s> halting his tall lank figure before her he raised a finger and levelled it at her bosom as though bringing an indictment against her beauty all i can say is these artistic people or whatever they call themselves they're as unreliable as they can be and my advice to you is don't you have too much to do with him <\s>
<s> irene smiled and in the curve of her lips was a strange provocation <\s>
<s> she seemed to have lost her deference <\s>
<s> her breast rose and fell as though with secret anger she drew her hands inwards from their rest on the arms of her chair until the tips of her fingers met and her dark eyes looked unfathomably at james <\s>
<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>

<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
<s> thus when he spoke it was in a sharper voice as if he had been awakened from a pleasant dream <\s>
<s> what d'you do with yourself all day <\s>
<s> you never come round to park lane <\s>
<s> she seemed to be making very lame excuses and james did not look at her <\s>
<s> he did not want to believe that she was really avoiding them it would mean too much <\s>
<s> i expect the fact is you haven't time he said you're always about with june <\s>
<s> i expect you're useful to her with her young man chaperoning and one thing and another <\s>
<s> they tell me she's never at home now your uncle jolyon he doesn't like it i fancy being left so much alone as he is <\s>
<s> they tell me she's always hanging about for this young bosinney i suppose he comes here every day <\s>
<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>

<s> now what do you think of him <\s>
<s> d'you think he knows his own mind <\s>
<s> he seems to me a poor thing <\s>
<s> i should say the grey mare was the better horse <\s>
<s> the colour deepened in irene's face and james watched her suspiciously <\s>
<s> perhaps you don't quite understand mr <\s>
<s> james hummed out why not you can see he's one of these artistic chaps <\s>
<s> they say he's clever they all think they're clever <\s>
<s> you know more about him than i do he added and again his suspicious glance rested on her <\s>
<s> he is designing a house for soames she said softly evidently trying to smooth things over <\s>
<s> that brings me to what i was going to say continued james i don't know what soames wants with a young man like that why doesn't he go to a first rate man <\s>
<s> james rose and took a turn with bent head <\s>
<s> that's it he said you young people you all stick together you all think you know best <\s>
<s> halting his tall lank figure before her he raised a finger and levelled it at her bosom as though bringing an indictment against her beauty all i can say is these artistic people or whatever they call themselves they're as unreliable as they can be and my advice to you is don't you have too much to do with him <\s>
<s> irene smiled and in the curve of her lips was a strange provocation <\s>
<s> she seemed to have lost her deference <\s>
<s> her breast rose and fell as though with secret anger she drew her hands inwards from their rest on the arms of her chair until the tips of her fingers met and her dark eyes looked unfathomably at james <\s>
<s> the latter gloomily scrutinized the floor <\s>
<s> i tell you my opinion he said it's a pity you haven't got a child to think about and occupy you <\s>
<s> a brooding look came instantly on irene's face and even james became conscious of the rigidity that took possession of her whole figure beneath the softness of its silk and lace clothing <\s>
<s> he was frightened by the effect he had produced and like most men with but little courage he sought at once to justify himself by bullying <\s>
<s> you don't seem to care about going about <\s>
<s> why don't you drive down to hurlingham with us <\s>
<s> and go to the theatre now and then <\s>
<s> at your time of life you ought to take an interest in things <\s>
<s> you're a young woman <\s>
<s> the brooding look darkened on her face he grew nervous <\s>
<s> well i know nothing about it he said nobody tells me anything <\s>
<s> soames ought to be able to take care of himself <\s>
<s> if he can't take care of himself he mustn't look to me that's all <\s>
<s> biting the corner of his forefinger he stole a cold sharp look at his daughter in law <\s>
<s> he encountered her eyes fixed on his own so dark and deep that he stopped and broke into a gentle perspiration <\s>
<s> well i must be going he said after a short pause and a minute later rose with a slight appearance of surprise as though he had expected to be asked to stop <\s>
<s> giving his hand to irene he allowed himself to be conducted to the door and let out into the street <\s>
<s> he would not have a cab he would walk irene was to say good night to soames for him and if she wanted a little gaiety well he would drive her down to richmond any day <\s>
<s> he walked home and going upstairs woke emily out of the first sleep she had had for four and twenty hours to tell her that it was his impression things were in a bad way at soames's on this theme he descanted for half an hour until at last saying that he would not sleep a wink he turned on his side and instantly began to snore <\s>
<s> in montpellier square soames who had come from the picture room stood invisible at the top of the stairs watching irene sort the letters brought by the last post <\s>
<s> she turned back into the drawing room but in a minute came out and stood as if listening <\s>
<s> then she came stealing up the stairs with a kitten in her arms <\s>
<s> he could see her face bent over the little beast which was purring against her neck <\s>
<s> why couldn't she look at him like that <\s>
<s> suddenly she saw him and her face changed <\s>
<s> any letters for me <\s>
<s> he stood aside and without another word she passed on into the bedroom <\s>
<s> chapter vii old jolyon's peccadillo old jolyon came out of lord's cricket ground that same afternoon with the intention of going home <\s>
<s> he had not reached hamilton terrace before he changed his mind and hailing a cab gave the driver an address in wistaria avenue <\s>
<s> he had taken a resolution <\s>
<s> june had hardly been at home at all that week she had given him nothing of her company for a long time past not in fact since she had become engaged to bosinney <\s>
<s> he never asked her for her company <\s>
<s> it was not his habit to ask people for things <\s>
<s> she had just that one idea now bosinney and his affairs and she left him stranded in his great house with a parcel of servants and not a soul to speak to from morning to night <\s>
<s> his club was closed for cleaning his boards in recess there was nothing therefore to take him into the city <\s>
<s> june had wanted him to go away she would not go herself because bosinney was in london <\s>
<s> but where was he to go by himself <\s>
<s> he could not go abroad alone the sea upset his liver he hated hotels <\s>
<s> roger went to a hydropathic he was not going to begin that at his time of life those new fangled places we're all humbug <\s>
<s> with such formulas he clothed to himself the desolation of his spirit the lines down his face deepening his eyes day by day looking forth with the melancholy which sat so strangely on a face wont to be strong and serene <\s>
<s> and so that afternoon he took this journey through st <\s>
<s> john's wood in the golden light that sprinkled the rounded green bushes of the acacia's before the little houses in the summer sunshine that seemed holding a revel over the little gardens and he looked about him with interest for this was a district which no forsyte entered without open disapproval and secret curiosity <\s>
<s> his cab stopped in front of a small house of that peculiar buff colour which implies a long immunity from paint <\s>
<s> it had an outer gate and a rustic approach <\s>
<s> he stepped out his bearing extremely composed his massive head with its drooping moustache and wings of white hair very upright under an excessively large top hat his glance firm a little angry <\s>
<s> he had been driven into this <\s>
<s> jolyon forsyte at home <\s>
<s> oh yes sir what name shall i say if you please sir <\s>
<s> old jolyon could not help twinkling at the little maid as he gave his name <\s>
<s> she seemed to him such a funny little toad <\s>
<s> and he followed her through the dark hall into a small double drawing room where the furniture was covered in chintz and the little maid placed him in a chair <\s>
<s> they're all in the garden sir if you'll kindly take a seat i'll tell them <\s>
<s> old jolyon sat down in the chintz covered chair and looked around him <\s>
<s> the whole place seemed to him as he would have expressed it pokey there was a certain he could not tell exactly what air of shabbiness or rather of making two ends meet about everything <\s>
<s> as far as he could see not a single piece of furniture was worth a five pound note <\s>
<s> the walls distempered rather a long time ago were decorated with water colour sketches across the ceiling meandered a long crack <\s>
<s> these little houses were all old second rate concerns he should hope the rent was under a hundred a year it hurt him more than he could have said to think of a forsyte his own son living in such a place <\s>
<s> the little maid came back <\s>
<s> would he please to go down into the garden <\s>
<s> old jolyon marched out through the french windows <\s>
<s> in descending the steps he noticed that they wanted painting <\s>
<s> but i can't get it at home <\s>
<s> i pay my cook sixty pounds a year but she can't give me a dinner like that <\s>
<s> he had as yet made no allusion to the building of the house nor did he when soames pleading the excuse of business betook himself to the room at the top where he kept his pictures <\s>
<s> james was left alone with his daughter in law <\s>
<s> the glow of the wine and of an excellent liqueur was still within him <\s>
<s> he felt quite warm towards her <\s>
<s> she was really a taking little thing she listened to you and seemed to understand what you were saying and while talking he kept examining her figure from her bronze coloured shoes to the waved gold of her hair <\s>
<s> she was leaning back in an empire chair her shoulders poised against the top her body flexibly straight and unsupported from the hips swaying when she moved as though giving to the arms of a lover <\s>
<s> her lips were smiling her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> it may have been a recognition of danger in the very charm of her attitude or a twang of digestion that caused a sudden dumbness to fall on james <\s>
<s> he did not remember ever having been quite alone with irene before <\s>
<s> and as he looked at her an odd feeling crept over him as though he had come across something strange and foreign <\s>
<s> now what was she thinking about sitting back like that <\s>
